# DNA Decode — AI/ML Project
<!-- project-schema: 0.1 -->

> Initialized 2026-05-11. Project ID: dna-decode-2026-05-11. Originating goal (verbatim user input): "use AI to decode and understand any DNA code which is a programming language written in the language of 3-5 proteins".

## Project Context
- **Project ID:** dna-decode-2026-05-11
- **Project root:** C:\Users\Farshad\PythonProjects\dna_decode
- **Captured:** 2026-05-11
- **Originating goal:** use AI to decode and understand any DNA code which is a programming language written in the language of 3-5 proteins
- **Refined goal (from 3c top-ranked candidate):** Build a biologically interpretable, research-grade evidence system for E. coli antibiotic resistance prediction (cipro/ceftriaxone/tet) with attribution to known resistance loci, validated under leave-one-Mash-clade-out CV. Multi-organism comparative work is a non-committed horizon track.
- **Horizon (months):** 12
- **Schema:** project-schema 0.1

## Empirical Concerns
- **Verdict:** FAIL
- **Check status:** attempted
- **Provisional:** NO
- **Findings:**
  - **Nucleotide-count error:** DNA is composed of 4 nucleotides (adenine A, thymine T, cytosine C, guanine G — the "ACGT" four-letter alphabet), not 3-5. The "3-5" figure has no biological correspondence at the nucleotide level. Source: genome.gov ACGT glossary; Wikipedia Nucleotide-base.
  - **Protein-vs-DNA conflation:** Proteins are downstream translation products of DNA (DNA → mRNA → ribosomal translation → protein), built from 20 standard amino acids encoded by 3-nucleotide codons. Proteins are NOT the alphabet of DNA. There are ~20K-100K distinct human proteins, none of which fits the "3-5" figure either. Source: Wikipedia Genetic code; DNA-and-RNA codon tables.
  - The "programming language" analogy is a common intuition pump, but the "language" of DNA is the 4-nucleotide alphabet at the encoding level + 64-codon table mapping codons to 20 amino acids + start/stop signals + regulatory elements (promoters, enhancers, etc.). It is NOT "written in 3-5 proteins."
- **Corrected factual premise:** Use AI to model relationships between DNA sequences (composed of 4 nucleotides: A, T, C, G, encoded into 64 codons that translate via the genetic code to 20 standard amino acids) and downstream biological function — regulatory activity, protein expression, phenotype.

## Project vs Research-Program
- **Verdict:** FAIL
- **Provisional:** NO
- **Classification:** research-program
- **Rationale:** Originating goal phrases scope as "any DNA code" (unbounded — all DNA from all organisms). No terminal condition, no measurable success criterion, no scoping by organism / chromosome / functional element / phenotype. Matches the unbounded-goal pattern flagged by Step 3b ("understand any X", "decode all Y"). A bounded sub-goal is required for project-shape work; the unbounded framing is research-program territory and would not converge in any practical horizon. Successful DNA-AI projects (AlphaFold, Enformer, Basenji, scBERT, DeepBind) all operate on narrowly-scoped sub-problems.

## Refinement Candidates
- **Verdict:** FAIL
- **Provisional:** NO
- **Refined-from:** corrected-factual-premise
- **Candidates:**
  1. **Regulatory-element prediction on chr21** — Build a tissue-specific gene-regulatory-element activity predictor for human chromosome 21 with ≥0.7 AUROC, using a transformer-based DNA model fine-tuned on ENCODE/Roadmap Epigenomics multi-tissue ChIP-seq + ATAC-seq, by 2026-09-30. **Top-ranked — selected for HTN decomposition.**
  2. **Non-coding-variant pathogenicity classifier** — Build a baseline classifier on a ClinVar-style benchmark achieving ≥0.65 AUC vs. Enformer-style pre-trained baselines, focused on interpreting which DNA-sequence features drive classifier decisions, by Q3 2026.
  3. **AlphaFold reproduction on a small protein family** — Reproduce AlphaFold-style protein-structure prediction on a 50-protein homologous family; benchmark predicted vs experimental structure on TM-score, by Q3 2026.
  4. **LLM-based gene-function annotation tool** — Take gene name as input; produce natural-language summary of gene function; evaluate against UniProt-curated descriptions on 100 held-out genes with ≥0.7 BLEU or human-rating ≥3/5 by Q4 2026.
  5. **Sequence-to-phenotype model on constrained dataset** — Train on GWAS-significant SNPs for one disease (e.g., Type 2 diabetes); benchmark against existing polygenic-risk-score methods, by Q4 2026.

## Goal Hierarchy
### Long-term (12+ months tier)
Build a biologically interpretable E. coli G2P (genotype-to-phenotype) prediction platform, starting with antibiotic resistance (ciprofloxacin + ceftriaxone + tetracycline) and expanding to multi-organism comparative genomics. Phase 1 ships a per-drug binary R/S classifier with attribution to known resistance loci; Phase 2 scales to N=150 with Mash-clade-out CV; Phase 3+ adds eukaryotic organisms and multimodal phenotype data.

### Mid-term (3-12 months) — REPLACED 2026-05-15 with Evidence Packet framework (per Pending Decisions row 8 framing reset; historical milestones — Phase 1 infra + 12-strain smoke + Stage 2 toolchain install — preserved in Decisions Made + Action Log)
| # | Evidence Packet | Success Criterion | Horizon |
|---|---|---|---|
| EP1 | cipro Stage 2 N=147/N=150 decision gate | Option-C: ≥5 pp NT-XGBoost lift over best classical AND top-K attribution includes ≥1 of {gyrA, parC, parE} under leave-one-Mash-clade-out CV | 2026-05/06 (gated on Stage 1 verdict; design + cohort + toolchain ready as of 2026-05-15) |
| EP2 | cef + tet smoke at 12-strain mini-cohort (parallel-fire data-shape probe) | NT not obviously worse than best classical by >15 pp on per-drug LOSO; mechanism-appropriate baseline classes per drug; falsifies cipro-derived architecture if signal-shape diverges | 2026-05/06 (post-Stage-1; EP2 design plan TBD per Pending Decisions row 9) |
| EP3 | Attribution biological-plausibility audit | Gene-level ISM recovery of mechanism-specific resistance loci (cipro: gyrA/parC/parE; cef: blaCTX-M / SHV / AmpC; tet: tetA/tetB/tetM); false-positive audit on synthetic-null baseline | 2026-06 (cipro audit gated on EP1 PASS; cef/tet gated on EP5; audit-runner build pending) |
| EP4 | Clade-shift calibration | Leave-one-Mash-clade-out test at N≥150 surfaces lineage leakage; H11a fires at production N (H11 superseded at N=12 — 12 singleton clades degenerate) | 2026-06 (part of EP1 verdict packet) |
| EP5 | cef Stage 2 + tet Stage 2 | NT beats best classical by ≥3 pp AUROC under LOSO at per-drug N≥100 (effective cohort size TBD per drug AST coverage) | 2026-07/08 (gated on EP2 signal-shape confirmation) |

## State Snapshot
### Assumptions
- User has Python ML background sufficient to fine-tune transformer models (confidence: medium — confirmed by Athena/RCA-Engine work in PythonProjects/)
- ENCODE / Roadmap Epigenomics data is publicly available and downloadable for chr21 multi-tissue tracks (confidence: high — well-documented public datasets)
- Pre-trained DNA-sequence transformers (Enformer, Basenji) have permissive licenses allowing fine-tuning (confidence: high — Enformer is Apache-2.0)
- Local hardware OR cloud budget allows non-trivial GPU training (confidence: low — not yet confirmed; see short-term action 5)
- 12-month horizon is realistic for a single-person regulatory-element prediction project to reach 0.7 AUROC baseline (confidence: medium — depends heavily on prior experience + compute access)
- The "AI to decode DNA" intent is genuinely about ML modeling, not about a different framing (e.g., natural-language explanation of genomics; gene-therapy automation) (confidence: medium — user's verbatim goal is ambiguous)

| 25 | Gene-presence AUROC=0.000 dual root cause confirmed empirically 2026-05-14: (a) `parse_gff3` extracted GFF3 `ID=` attribute into `gene_id` → strain-unique vocabulary → 0% cross-strain LOSO overlap → all-zero test rows; (b) on all-zero rows XGBoost predicts training class prior → on balanced LOSO cohort the prior always inverts vs held-out label → perfect rank inversion AUROC=0.000. Fix shipped: added `gene_symbol` column to AnnotationTable (populated from `gene=` attribute); smoke runner prefers it; added `INDETERMINATE_IDENTIFIER_OOV` guardrail thresholding on median per-fold vocab overlap < 20%. Post-fix overlap = 10.84% on the 12-strain cohort → correctly tagged INDETERMINATE because RefSeq GFF3 only carries `gene=` for ~11% of CDSs. NT and k-mer variants unaffected. | scripts/diagnose_gene_presence_auroc.py + smoke_gate_12strain_cipro_2026-05-14.md | high | 2026-05-14 |
| 26 | PCA + UMAP of 12-strain NT embeddings: PC1 captures 80.7% variance but R/S mean separation on PC1 is only 0.024 (within-noise). NT classifier achieves AUROC=0.750 despite no 2D-projection separation — resistance signal lives in higher-D structure NT learned, not on the dominant variance axes. All 12 MLSTs unique. Plot at `wiki/pca_umap_12strain_cipro_2026-05-14.png`. Falsifies H15 (no by-eye separation) but does NOT undermine the classifier verdict — the 2D projection is informational not decisive. | scripts/plot_nt_embeddings_pca_umap.py output | high | 2026-05-14 |

- Compute-budget ceiling (local GPU available? cloud spend approved?)
- User's prior bioinformatics depth (Python ML known; genomics-specific tooling unknown)

## Bellman-Inspired Decision Frame

Per D5: surfaces the Bellman cognitive frame at the architecture level. v0.1 populates this at init; v0.2's `/project-step` reads from it to decide next actions. v0.1 does NOT iterate over the frame — it sets it up.

### Current state (one-line summary) — REFRESHED 2026-06-19 (AMR track BANKED; genome-map honesty tool GO + productized)
**The deterministic AMR decoder is the banked terminal product of the public-label AMR track** (reproducibility freeze 2026-06-13, `wiki/reproducibility_freeze_2026-06-13.md`): 10 provenance-disjoint SCORED cells, lineage-disclosed, frozen. Every public-label expansion is CLOSED with recorded negatives (`wiki/negative_results_map_2026-06-13.md` — 8 reusable rejection gates; binding constraint is LABELS, not models). Since the freeze: external-cohort re-validation arm + Oxford MIC ingester (2026-06-15), TMP-SMX experimental overlay (2026-06-16), first M. tuberculosis AMR cell (`organism_rules/`, 2026-06-17, BLOCKED-gated pending data runs).

**Genome-map v1 "Bakta honesty report" shipped + verdict GO (2026-06-18) and PRODUCTIZED (2026-06-19).** The achievable, label-free form of the north star ("DNA → what its parts do"): point at ONE microbial genome → an honest evidence-tiered per-feature map (4 tiers; phenotype only behind a validated-determinant wall; DB-labelled `unknown_under_bakta_db_light`). NOT a learned predictor (that arm stays a closed negative). `dna_decode/genome_map/` + `scripts/genome_map.py` (single-genome CLI), `genome_map_spike.py`, `genome_map_tool_surface.py`; 84 tests; frozen AMR surface byte-unchanged. Live 3-genome spike GO (E. coli 6.1% unknown/23 determinant-phenotype incl. a real tandem blaTEM-20 array; K. pneumoniae 8.6%; Gemmata 67.9%). First end-to-end Bakta proof on this host.

**Two non-foreclosed forward paths, both a USER decision (neither an executor task):** (1) ACQUISITION of a non-public wet-lab/clinical label source (clears the label gates by construction; anchor `wiki/next_epoch_idea_anchor_prompt_2026-06-13.md`); (2) PROSPECTIVE-LOCK validation of the frozen decoder against later-arriving independent data. Genome-map next-investment (catalog integration at scale; richer homology tiers) is also a user investment call. **Do NOT reopen public-label AMR expansion or the embedding/MIC tracks — closed with negatives.** (Correction 2026-06-19: the EP8 Path B Arabidopsis embedding run is NOT pending GPU work — it RAN + FALSIFIED 2026-06-12, the 3rd de-confounded embedding failure across the kingdom boundary; the eukaryotic embedding arm is a CLOSED NEGATIVE, not parked. The earlier "lives on the Precision 7780" framing in this block + the genome-map handoff was stale.)

### Target state / terminal condition

Parked horizon tracks (no ledger commitment): 2nd-organism portability, MIC continuous head, pan-genome graph, multimodal DNA+image gated on paired-dataset existence (≥1000 paired strains).

### Progress proxy
- **v0.1 metric:** `unknowns-retired` count + `gates-passed` count (raw counts, unweighted). At init: unknowns-retired = 0; gates-passed = 0 (3 of 3 goal-normalization sub-gates returned FAIL → no "passed" gates yet, the FAILs are intentional and successful catches).
- **v0.2+:** weighted combination of unknowns-retired, gates-passed, evidence-confidence-improved, hypotheses-falsified.

### Re-evaluation trigger
- **Default:** re-run `/project-state` after any action class fires (auto-append to Action Log triggers stale-state check)
- **Manual override:** user invokes `/project-state dna-decode-2026-05-11` at any time
- **v0.2+:** automated trigger when N actions fire OR T days elapse OR a hypothesis falsifies (TBD)

- `research` — auto (delegate to /research / /athena-research / /research-verify)
- `write-plan` — auto (delegate to /technical-plan / /save-plan)
- `edit-local-code` — REQUIRES per-action human approval
- `run-tests` — auto if local + sandboxed
- `ask-user` — auto
- `stop` — auto
